focus = {
	id = PRU_organize_future_elections
    mutually_exclusive = { focus = PRU_look_to_the_past }
	icon = GFX_goal_PRU_peru_republic
	x = 20
	y = 0

	cost = 7.2	#50 days, not 42

	allow_branch = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = obsolete_focus_branches_visibility
					option = HIDE
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = PRU_look_to_the_past
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 10
	}

	completion_reward = {
		add_political_power = 25
		add_stability = 0.05
		country_event = { hours = 4 id = peru.1 }
        hidden_effect = {
			PRU = { country_event = { days = 35 id = peru.56 } }	
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }
}

focus = {
	id = PRU_ask_for_enter_to_comintern
	prerequisite = { focus =PRU_the_teachings_the_amauta focus=PRU_give_asylum_to_the_jews}
	icon = GFX_focus_chi_mission_to_the_soviet_union
	x = -4
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = PRU_the_teachings_the_amauta
    mutually_exclusive = {
            focus = PRU_left_and_right_united
        }
	cost = 10
	available = {
		OR = {
		has_completed_focus = PRU_the_teachings_the_amauta
		 if = {
			limit = {has_country_leader = { character = PRU_arturo_peralta ruling_only = yes }}
			has_completed_focus = PRU_workers_rights_act
		}  
	    }
		is_subject = no
		is_in_faction = no
		OR = {
			communism > 0.5
			has_government = communism
		}
		OR = {
			SOV = {
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				has_government = communism
				has_capitulated = no
				is_faction_leader = yes
				has_opinion = {
					target = ROOT
					value > -11
				}
			}
			any_other_country = {
				is_major = yes
				has_government = communism
				is_faction_leader = yes
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				has_opinion = {
					target = ROOT
					value > -11
				}
			}
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 7
	}

	completion_reward = {
		if = {
			limit = {has_country_leader = { character = PRU_arturo_peralta ruling_only = yes }}
			swap_ideas = {
			  remove_idea = PRU_weak_republic_2
		      add_idea = PRU_communist_republic
			}
		} 
		if = {
			limit = {
				SOV = {
					has_government = communism
					is_faction_leader = yes
					has_capitulated = no
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
				NOT = {
					any_other_country = {
						is_in_faction_with = SOV
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}

			SOV = {
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = PRU modifier = large_increase }
				country_event = { days = 1 id =generic.2 }
			}

		}

		else = {
			get_best_alliance_match_communism_effect = yes
			var:best_leader = {
				country_event = generic.2
			}
		}

	}
	search_filters = {FOCUS_FILTER_ALLIANCE}
}

					}
